capita</div></th><td>\n$16,332<sup id="cite_ref-imf2_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-imf2-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Gini_coefficient" title="Gini coefficient">Gini</a>&#160;<span style="font-weight:normal;">(2013)</span></th><td>\n46.8<sup id="cite_ref-gini-index_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gini-index-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><br /><span style="white-space:nowrap;"><span style="color:darkred">high</span></span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Human_Development_Index" title="Human Development Index">HDI</a>&#160;<span style="font-weight:normal;">(2017)</span></th><td>\n<img alt="Increase" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Increase2.svg/11px-Increase2.svg.png" href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_Human_Development_Index" title="List of countries by Human Development Index">62nd</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Currency</th><td>\n<a Time">UTC</a>+4</span> (not observed)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Left-_and_right-hand_traffic" title="Left- and right-hand traffic">Drives on the</a></th><td>\nleft</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Telephone_numbers_in_Seychelles" title="Telephone numbers in Seychelles">Calling code</a></th><td>\n<a href="/wiki/%2B248" class="mw-redirect" title="+248">+248</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/ISO_3166" title="ISO 3166">ISO 3166 code</a></th><td>\n<a href="/wiki/ISO_3166-2:SC" title="ISO 3166-2:SC">SC</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Country_code_top-level_domain" title="Country code top-level domain">Internet TLD</a></th><td>\n<a href="/wiki/.sc" title=".sc">.sc</a></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Seychelles</b> (<span class="nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span><span title="/e\xc9\xaa/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;face&#39;">e\xc9\xaa</span><span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\xcb\x88</span><span title="/\xca\x83/: &#39;sh&#39; in &#39;shy&#39;">\xca\x83</span><span title="/\xc9\x9b/: &#39;e&#39; in &#39;dress&#39;">\xc9\x9b</span><span title="&#39;l&#39; in &#39;lie&#39;">l</span><span title="&#39;z&#39; in &#39;zoom&#39;">z</span></span>/</a></span><small class="nowrap">&#160;(<span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:En-us-Seychelles.ogg" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20" /></a>&#160;</span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/4/4f/En-us-Seychelles.ogg" class="internal" title="En-us-Seychelles.ogg">listen</a></span></span>)</small></span> <a href="/wiki/Help:Pronunciation_respelling_key" title="Help:Pronunciation respelling key"><i title="English pronunciation respelling">say-<span style="font-size:90%">SHELZ</span></i></a>; French: <small></small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/French" title="Help:IPA/French">[se\xca\x83\xc9\x9bl]</a></span>), officially the <b>Republic of Seychelles</b> (French: <i lang="fr">R\xc3\xa9publique des Seychelles</i>; <a href="/wiki/Seychellois_Creole" title="Seychellois Creole">Creole</a>: <i>Repiblik Sesel</i>), is an <a href="/wiki/Archipelago" title="Archipelago">archipelago</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign state</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian Ocean</a>. The capital of the 115-<a href="/wiki/Island_country" title="Island country">island country</a>, <a href="/wiki/Victoria,_Seychelles" title="Victoria, Seychelles">Victoria</a>, lies 1,500 kilometres (932&#160;mi) east of mainland <a href="/wiki/East_Africa" title="East Africa">East Africa</a>. Other nearby island countries and territories include <a href="/wiki/Comoros" title="Comoros">Comoros</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mayotte" title="Mayotte">Mayotte</a> (<a href="/wiki/Region_of_France" class="mw-redirect" title="Region of France">region of France</a>), <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascar</a>, <a href="/wiki/R%C3%A9union" title="R\xc3\xa9union">R\xc3\xa9union</a> (region of France) and <a href="/wiki/Mauritius" title="Mauritius">Mauritius</a> to the south. With a population of roughly 94,228, it has the <a href="/wiki/List_of_African_countries_by_population" title="List of African countries by population">smallest population of any sovereign African country</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Seychelles is a member of the <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Southern_African_Development_Community" title="Southern African Development Community">Southern African Development Community</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth of Nations</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>. After proclamation of independence from the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> in 1976, Seychelles has developed from a largely agricultural society to a market-based diversified economy, with agriculture being supplanted by rapidly rising <a href="/wiki/Service_sector" class="mw-redirect" title="Service sector">service</a> and <a href="/wiki/Public_sector" title="Public sector">public sectors</a> as well as <a href="/wiki/Tourism" title="Tourism">tourism</a>. Since 1976, nominal GDP output has increased nearly sevenfold and the <a href="/wiki/Purchasing_power_parity" title="Purchasing power parity">purchasing power parity</a> nearly sixteenfold. In recent years, the government has encouraged foreign investment in order to upgrade these sectors. Today, Seychelles boasts the highest <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(nominal)_per_capita" title="List of countries by GDP (nominal) per capita">nominal per capita GDP</a> in Africa, excluding the <a href="/wiki/Region_of_France" class="mw-redirect" title="Region of France">French regions</a>. It is one of only a handful of countries in Africa with a high <a href="/wiki/List_of_African_countries_by_Human_Development_Index" title="List of African countries by Human Development Index">Human Development Index</a>. Despite the country\'s newfound economic prosperity, poverty remains widespread due to a high level of <a href="/wiki/Income_inequality" class="mw-redirect" title="Income inequality">income inequality</a>, one of the highest in the world, and unequal <a href="/wiki/Wealth_distribution" class="mw-redirect" title="Wealth distribution">wealth distribution</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>\n<ul>\n<li class="toctext">Education</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-19"><a href="#Cuisine"><span class="tocnumber">6.2</span> <span class="toctext">Cuisine</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-25"><a href="#Incarceration"><span class="tocnumber">7.2</span> <span class="toctext">Incarceration</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-26"><a class="toctext">References</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-29"><a href="#External_links"><span class="tocnumber">10</span> <span class="toctext">External links</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Seychelles&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/History_of_Seychelles" title="History of Seychelles">History of Seychelles</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Victoria_Seychelles_1900s.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Victoria_Seychelles_1900s.jpg/220px-Victoria_Seychelles_1900s.jpg" width="220" height="170" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Victoria_Seychelles_1900s.jpg/330px-Victoria_Seychelles_1900s.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Victoria_Seychelles_1900s.jpg/440px-Victoria_Seychelles_1900s.jpg 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="463" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Victoria_Seychelles_1900s.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Victoria, Seychelles 1900s</div></div></div>\n<p>The Seychelles were uninhabited throughout most of recorded history. Some scholars assume that <a href="/wiki/Austronesian_people" class="mw-redirect" title="Austronesian people">Austronesian</a> seafarers and later <a href="/wiki/Maldive_Islands" title="Maldive Islands">Maldivian</a> and Arab traders were the first to visit the uninhabited Seychelles. This assumption is based on the discovery of tombs, visible until 1910.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> The earliest recorded sighting by Europeans took place in 1502 by the Portuguese Admiral <a href="/wiki/Vasco_da_Gama" title="Vasco da Gama">Vasco da Gama</a>, who passed through the <a href="/wiki/Amirantes" class="mw-redirect" title="Amirantes">Amirantes</a> and named them after himself (islands of the Admiral). The earliest recorded landing was in January 1609, by the crew of the "Ascension" under Captain <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Sharpeigh" title="Alexander Sharpeigh">Alexander Sharpeigh</a> during the fourth voyage of the British <a href="/wiki/East_India_Company" title="East India Company">East India Company</a>.\n</p><p>A transit point for trade between Africa and Asia, the islands were occasionally used by <a href="/wiki/Pirates" class="mw-redirect" title="Pirates">pirates</a> until the French began to take control starting in 1756 when a Stone of Possession was laid on <a href="/wiki/Mah%C3%A9,_Seychelles" title="Mah\xc3\xa9, Seychelles">Mah\xc3\xa9</a> by Captain <a href="/wiki/Corneille_Nicholas_Morphey" title="Corneille Nicholas Morphey">Nicholas Morphey</a>. The islands were named after <a href="/wiki/Jean_Moreau_de_S%C3%A9chelles" title="Jean Moreau de S\xc3\xa9chelles">Jean Moreau de S\xc3\xa9chelles</a>, <a href="/wiki/Louis_XV" class="mw-redirect" title="Louis XV">Louis XV</a>\'s Minister of Finance.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The British controlled the islands between 1794 and 1810. Jean Baptiste Qu\xc3\xa9au de Quincy, French administrator of Seychelles during the years of war with the United Kingdom, declined to resist when armed enemy warships arrived. Instead, he successfully negotiated the status of capitulation to Britain which gave the settlers a privileged position of neutrality.\n</p><p>Britain eventually assumed full control upon the surrender of <a href="/wiki/Mauritius" title="Mauritius">Mauritius</a> in 1810, formalised in 1814 at the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Paris_(1814)" title="Treaty of Paris (1814)">Treaty of Paris</a>. Seychelles became a <a href="/wiki/Crown_colony" title="Crown colony">crown colony</a> separate from Mauritius in 1903. Elections were held in 1966 and 1970.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Independence">Independence</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Seychelles&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Independence">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Independence was granted in 1976 as a republic within the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-History_of_Seychelles_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-History_of_Seychelles-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> In the 1970s Seychelles was "the place to be seen, a playground for film stars and the international jet set".<sup id="cite_ref-telegraph.co.uk_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraph.co.uk-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> In 1977, a <a href="/wiki/Coup_d%27%C3%A9tat" title="Coup d&#39;\xc3\xa9tat">coup d\'\xc3\xa9tat</a> by <a href="/wiki/France_Albert_Ren%C3%A9" class="mw-redirect" title="France Albert Ren\xc3\xa9">France Albert Ren\xc3\xa9</a> ousted the first president of the republic, <a href="/wiki/James_Mancham" title="James Mancham">James Mancham</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-africanhistory.about.com_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-africanhistory.about.com-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Ren\xc3\xa9 discouraged over-dependence on tourism and declared that he wanted "to keep the Seychelles for the Seychellois".<sup id="cite_ref-telegraph.co.uk_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraph.co.uk-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The 1979 constitution declared a socialist one-party state, which lasted until 1991.\n</p><p>In the 1980s there were a series of coup attempts against President Ren\xc3\xa9, some of which were supported by South Africa. In 1981, <a href="/wiki/Mike_Hoare" class="mw-redirect" title="Mike Hoare">Mike Hoare</a> led a team of 43 South African mercenaries masquerading as holidaying rugby players in the <a href="/wiki/1981_Seychelles_coup_d%27%C3%A9tat_attempt" title="1981 Seychelles coup d&#39;\xc3\xa9tat attempt">1981 Seychelles coup d\'\xc3\xa9tat attempt</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraph.co.uk_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraph.co.uk-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> There was a gun battle at the airport, and most of the mercenaries later escaped in a hijacked <a href="/wiki/Air_India" title="Air India">Air India</a> plane.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraph.co.uk_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraph.co.uk-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> The leader of this hijacking was German mercenary D. Clodo, a former member of the Rhodesian SAS.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Clodo later stood trial in South Africa (where he was acquitted) as well as in his home country Germany for air-piracy.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 1986, an attempted coup led by the Seychelles Minister of Defence, Ogilvy Berlouis, caused President Ren\xc3\xa9 to request assistance from India. In <a href="/wiki/Operation_Flowers_are_Blooming" title="Operation Flowers are Blooming">Operation Flowers are Blooming</a>, the Indian naval vessel <a href="/wiki/INS_Vindhyagiri" title="INS Vindhyagiri">INS Vindhyagiri</a> arrived in Port Victoria to help avert the coup.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The first draft of a new constitution failed to receive the requisite 60% of voters in 1992, but an amended version was approved in 1993.\n</p><p>In January 2013, Seychelles declared a state of emergency; the tropical cyclone Felleng caused torrential rain, and flooding and landslides destroyed hundreds of houses.<sup id="cite_ref-UN_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UN-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AL_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AL-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Politics">Politics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Seychelles&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Politics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Victoria.jpeg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Victoria.jpeg/220px-Victoria.jpeg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Victoria.jpeg/330px-Victoria.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Victoria.jpeg/440px-Victoria.jpeg 2x" data-file-width="935" data-file-height="702" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Victoria.jpeg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Victoria,_Seychelles" title="Victoria, Seychelles">Victoria</a>, the capital of Seychelles</div></div></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Seychelles" title="Politics of Seychelles">Politics of Seychelles</a></div>\n<p>The Seychelles president, who is <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">head of state</a> and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_government" title="Head of government">head of government</a>, is elected by popular vote for a five-year term of office. The cabinet is presided over and appointed by the president, subject to the approval of a majority of the legislature.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Unicameral" class="mw-redirect" title="Unicameral">unicameral</a> Seychellois parliament, <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(Seychelles)" title="National Assembly (Seychelles)">the National Assembly</a> or <i>Assembl\xc3\xa9e Nationale</i>, consists of 34 members, 25 of whom are elected directly by popular vote, while the remaining nine seats are appointed proportionally according to the percentage of votes received by each party. All members serve five-year terms.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Seychelles" title="Supreme Court of Seychelles">Supreme Court of Seychelles</a>, created in 1903, is the highest trial court in Seychelles and the first court of appeal from all the lower courts and tribunals. The highest court of law in Seychelles is the Seychelles Court of Appeal, which is the court of final appeal in the country.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Political_culture">Political culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Seychelles&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Political culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:James_Michel_in_meeting.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/James_Michel_in_meeting.jpg/220px-James_Michel_in_meeting.jpg" width="220" height="170" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/James_Michel_in_meeting.jpg/330px-James_Michel_in_meeting.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/James_Michel_in_meeting.jpg/440px-James_Michel_in_meeting.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1648" data-file-height="1276" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:James_Michel_in_meeting.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Former President <a href="/wiki/James_Michel" title="James Michel">James Michel</a> in his office in <a href="/wiki/Victoria,_Seychelles" title="Victoria, Seychelles">Victoria</a>, 2009</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Se-map.gif" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Se-map.gif/220px-Se-map.gif" width="220" height="237" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/77/Se-map.gif 1.5x" data-file-width="328" data-file-height="353" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Se-map.gif" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map of Seychelles</div></div></div>\n<p>Seychelles\'s previous president <a href="/wiki/France_Albert_Ren%C3%A9" class="mw-redirect" title="France Albert Ren\xc3\xa9">France Albert Ren\xc3\xa9</a> came to power after his supporters overthrew the first president <a href="/wiki/James_Mancham" title="James Mancham">James Mancham</a> on 5 June 1977 in a <a href="/wiki/Coup_d%27%C3%A9tat" title="Coup d&#39;\xc3\xa9tat">coup d\'\xc3\xa9tat</a> and installed him as president. Ren\xc3\xa9 was at that time the prime minister.<sup id="cite_ref-Seychelles_Nation_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Seychelles_Nation-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Reuters_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Reuters-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Agence_France-Presse_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Agence_France-Presse-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Ren\xc3\xa9 ruled as a <a href="/wiki/Strongman_(politics)" title="Strongman (politics)">strongman</a> under a <a href="/wiki/Socialist" class="mw-redirect" title="Socialist">socialist</a> <a href="/wiki/One-party_system" class="mw-redirect" title="One-party system">one-party system</a> until in 1993, when he was forced to introduce a multi-party system. He stepped down in 2004 in favour of his vice-president, <a href="/wiki/James_Michel" title="James Michel">James Michel</a>, who was re-elected in 2006 and again in 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-Seychelles_Nation_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Seychelles_Nation-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Reuters_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Reuters-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Agence_France-Presse_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Agence_France-Presse-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> On 28 September 2016, the Office of the President announced that Michel would step down effective 16 October, and that Vice President Danny Faure would complete the rest of Michel\'s term.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The primary political parties are the ruling socialist <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Party_(Seychelles)" title="People&#39;s Party (Seychelles)">People\'s Party</a> (PP), known until 2009 as the Seychelles People\'s Progressive Front (SPPF), and the <a href="/wiki/Social_liberalism" title="Social liberalism">socially liberal</a> <a href="/wiki/Seychelles_National_Party" title="Seychelles National Party">Seychelles National Party</a> (SNP).<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Foreign_relations">Foreign relations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Seychelles&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Foreign relations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Seychelles" title="Foreign relations of Seychelles">Foreign relations of Seychelles</a></div>\n<p>Seychelles is a member of the African Union, the francophone <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean_Commission" title="Indian Ocean Commission">Indian Ocean Commission</a> (IOC), <a href="/wiki/La_Francophonie" class="mw-redirect" title="La Francophonie">La Francophonie</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Southern_African_Development_Community" title="Southern African Development Community">Southern African Development Community</a> (SADC) and the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Administrative_divisions">Administrative divisions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Seychelles&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Administrative divisions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Districts_of_Seychelles" title="Districts of Seychelles">Districts of Seychelles</a></div>\n<p>Seychelles is divided into twenty-six administrative regions comprising all of the inner islands. Eight of the districts make up the capital of Seychelles and are referred to as Greater <a href="/wiki/Victoria,_Seychelles" title="Victoria, Seychelles">Victoria</a>. Another 14 districts are considered the rural part of the main island of <a href="/wiki/Mah%C3%A9,_Seychelles" title="Mah\xc3\xa9, Seychelles">Mah\xc3\xa9</a> with two districts on <a href="/wiki/Praslin" title="Praslin">Praslin</a> and one on <a href="/wiki/La_Digue" title="La Digue">La Digue</a> which also includes respective satellite islands. The rest of the <a href="/wiki/Outer_Islands_(Seychelles)" title="Outer Islands (Seychelles)">Outer Islands</a> (<i><i lang="fr" title="French language text">\xc3\x8eles Eloign\xc3\xa9es</i></i>) are the last district, recently created by the tourism ministry.\n</p>\n<div>\n\n&#32;\n<table class="multicol" role="presentation" style="border-collapse: collapse; padding: 0; border: 0; (Anse R\xc3\xa9union)</li></ul>\n<p>&#32;\n</p>\n</td></tr></tbody></table></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">Geography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Seychelles&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Geography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_Seychelles" title="Geography of Seychelles">Geography of Seychelles</a></div>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.</span>  <small><i>(February 2017)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:802px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Praslin_vom_Nid_d%27Aigle.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Praslin_vom_Nid_d%27Aigle.jpg/800px-Praslin_vom_Nid_d%27Aigle.jpg" width="800" height="271" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Praslin_vom_Nid_d%27Aigle.jpg/1200px-Praslin_vom_Nid_d%27Aigle.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Praslin_vom_Nid_d%27Aigle.jpg/1600px-Praslin_vom_Nid_d%27Aigle.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5000" data-file-height="1692" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Praslin_vom_Nid_d%27Aigle.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>View of <a href="/wiki/Praslin" title="Praslin">Praslin</a>, the second largest island of the Seychelles</div></div></div></div>\n<p>An island nation, Seychelles is located in the Indian Ocean, northeast of <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascar</a> and about 1,600&#160;km (994&#160;mi) east of <a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>. The archipelago consists of 115 islands. The majority of the islands are uninhabited, with many dedicated as nature reserves.\n</p><p>A group of 42 islands, referred to as the inland islands, has a total area of 244&#160;km<sup>2</sup>, comprising 54% of the total land area of the Seychelles and 98% of the entire population.\n</p><p>The islands are divided into groups as follows.\n</p><p>There are 45 granite-based islands known as the <a href="/wiki/Granitic_Seychelles" title="Granitic Seychelles">Granitic Seychelles</a>. These are in descending order of size: <a href="/wiki/Mah%C3%A9,_Seychelles" title="Mah\xc3\xa9, Seychelles">Mah\xc3\xa9</a>, <a href="/wiki/Praslin" title="Praslin">Praslin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Silhouette_Island" title="Silhouette Island">Silhouette Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/La_Digue" title="La Digue">La Digue</a>, <a href="/wiki/Curieuse" class="mw-redirect" title="Curieuse">Curieuse</a>, <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9licit%C3%A9_Island" title="F\xc3\xa9licit\xc3\xa9 Island">F\xc3\xa9licit\xc3\xa9</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fr%C3%A9gate_Island" title="Fr\xc3\xa9gate Island">Fr\xc3\xa9gate</a>, Ste-Anne, North, Cerf, Marianne, Grand S\xc5\x93ur, Th\xc3\xa9r\xc3\xa8se, Aride, Conception, Petite S\xc5\x93ur, Cousin, Cousine, Long, R\xc3\xa9cif, Round (Praslin), Anonyme, Mamelles, <a href="/wiki/Moyenne_Island" title="Moyenne Island">Moyenne</a>, Eden, \xc3\x8ele Soleil, Romainville, \xc3\x8ele aux Vaches Marines, L\'Islette, Beacon (\xc3\x8ele S\xc3\xa8che), <a href="/wiki/Cach%C3%A9e_Island" title="Cach\xc3\xa9e Island">Cach\xc3\xa9e</a>, Cocos, Round (Mah\xc3\xa9), L\'Ilot Fr\xc3\xa9gate, Booby, Chauve-Souris (Mah\xc3\xa9), Chauve-Souris (Praslin), \xc3\x8ele La Fouche, Hodoul, L\'Ilot, Rat, Souris, St. Pierre (Praslin), Zav\xc3\xa9, Harrison Rocks (Grand Rocher).\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Anse_Source_d%27Argent_2-La_Digue.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Anse_Source_d%27Argent_2-La_Digue.jpg/220px-Anse_Source_d%27Argent_2-La_Digue.jpg" width="220" height="158" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Anse_Source_d%27Argent_2-La_Digue.jpg/330px-Anse_Source_d%27Argent_2-La_Digue.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Anse_Source_d%27Argent_2-La_Digue.jpg/440px-Anse_Source_d%27Argent_2-La_Digue.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2000" data-file-height="1435" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Anse_Source_d%27Argent_2-La_Digue.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beach of Anse Source d\'Argent on the island of <a href="/wiki/La_Digue" title="La Digue">La Digue</a></div></div></div>\n<p>There are two coral sand <a href="/wiki/Cay" title="Cay">cays</a> north of the granitics: <a href="/wiki/Denis_Island" title="Denis Island">Denis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bird_Island,_Seychelles" title="Bird Island, Seychelles">Bird</a>.\n</p><p>There are two <a href="/wiki/Coral_island" title="Coral island">coral islands</a> south of the Granitics: <a href="/wiki/Co%C3%ABtivy_Island" title="Co\xc3\xabtivy Island">Co\xc3\xabtivy</a> and <a href="/wiki/%C3%8Ele_Platte" title="\xc3\x8ele Platte">Platte</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Anse_Lazio_beach_Praslin_Seychelles.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Anse_Lazio_beach_Praslin_Seychelles.jpg/220px-Anse_Lazio_beach_Praslin_Seychelles.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Anse_Lazio_beach_Praslin_Seychelles.jpg/330px-Anse_Lazio_beach_Praslin_Seychelles.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Anse_Lazio_beach_Praslin_Seychelles.jpg/440px-Anse_Lazio_beach_Praslin_Seychelles.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Anse_Lazio_beach_Praslin_Seychelles.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beach of <a href="/wiki/Anse_Lazio" title="Anse Lazio">Anse Lazio</a> on the island of <a href="/wiki/Praslin" title="Praslin">Praslin</a></div></div></div>\n<p>There are 29 coral islands in the <a href="/wiki/Amirantes" class="mw-redirect" title="Amirantes">Amirantes group</a>, west of the granitics: <a href="/wiki/Desroches" class="mw-redirect" title="Desroches">Desroches</a>, Poivre Atoll (comprising three islands\xe2\x80\x94Poivre, Florentin and South Island), Alphonse, D\'Arros, St. Joseph Atoll (comprising 14 islands\xe2\x80\x94St. Joseph \xc3\x8ele aux Fouquets, Resource, Petit Carcassaye, Grand Carcassaye, Benjamin, Bancs Ferrari, Chiens, P\xc3\xa9licans, Vars, \xc3\x8ele Paul, Banc de Sable, Banc aux Cocos and \xc3\x8ele aux Poules), Marie Louise, Desn\xc5\x93ufs, African Banks (comprising two islands\xe2\x80\x94African Banks and South Island), R\xc3\xa9mire, St. Fran\xc3\xa7ois, Boudeuse, \xc3\x89toile, Bijoutier.\n</p><p>There are 13 coral islands in the <a href="/wiki/Farquhar_Group" title="Farquhar Group">Farquhar Group</a>, south-southwest of the Amirantes: <a href="/wiki/Farquhar_Atoll" title="Farquhar Atoll">Farquhar Atoll</a> (comprising 10 islands\xe2\x80\x94Bancs de Sable, D\xc3\xa9pos\xc3\xa9s, \xc3\x8ele aux Go\xc3\xablettes, Lapins, \xc3\x8ele du Milieu, North Manaha, South Manaha, Middle Manaha, North Island and South Island), Providence Atoll (comprising two islands\xe2\x80\x94Providence and Bancs Providence) and St Pierre.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Seychelles_017.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Seychelles_017.JPG/220px-Seychelles_017.JPG" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Seychelles_017.JPG/330px-Seychelles_017.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Seychelles_017.JPG/440px-Seychelles_017.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="900" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Seychelles_017.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mah\xc3\xa9 Island</div></div></div>\n<p>There are 67 <a href="/wiki/Raised_coral_atoll" title="Raised coral atoll">raised coral islands</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Aldabra_Group" title="Aldabra Group">Aldabra Group</a>, west of the Farquhar Group: <a href="/wiki/Aldabra_Atoll" class="mw-redirect" title="Aldabra Atoll">Aldabra Atoll</a> (comprising 46 islands\xe2\x80\x94Grande Terre, Picard, Polymnie, Malabar, \xc3\x8ele Michel, \xc3\x8ele Esprit, \xc3\x8ele aux Moustiques, Ilot Parc, Ilot \xc3\x89mile, Ilot Yangue, Ilot Magnan, \xc3\x8ele Lanier, Champignon des Os, Euphrate, Grand Mentor, Grand Ilot, Gros Ilot Gionnet, Gros Ilot S\xc3\xa9same, H\xc3\xa9ron Rock, Hide Island, \xc3\x8ele aux Aigrettes, \xc3\x8ele aux C\xc3\xa8dres, \xc3\x8eles Chalands, \xc3\x8ele Fangame, \xc3\x8ele H\xc3\xa9ron, \xc3\x8ele Michel, \xc3\x8ele Squacco, \xc3\x8ele Sylvestre, \xc3\x8ele Verte, Ilot D\xc3\xa9der, Ilot du Sud, Ilot du Milieu, Ilot du Nord, Ilot Dubois, Ilot Macoa, Ilot Marquoix, Ilots Ni\xc3\xa7ois, Ilot Salade, Middle Row Island, Noddy Rock, North Row Island, Petit Mentor, Petit Mentor Endans, Petits Ilots, Pink Rock and Table Ronde), <a href="/wiki/Assumption_Island" title="Assumption Island">Assumption Island</a>, Astove and <a href="/wiki/Cosmoledo_Atoll" class="mw-redirect" title="Cosmoledo Atoll">Cosmoledo Atoll</a> (comprising 19 islands\xe2\x80\x94Menai, \xc3\x8ele du Nord (West North), \xc3\x8ele Nord-Est (East North), \xc3\x8ele du Trou, Go\xc3\xa9lettes, Grand Polyte, Petit Polyte, Grand \xc3\x8ele (Wizard), Pagode, \xc3\x8ele du Sud-Ouest (South), \xc3\x8ele aux Moustiques, \xc3\x8ele Baleine, \xc3\x8ele aux Chauve-Souris, \xc3\x8ele aux Macaques, \xc3\x8ele aux Rats, \xc3\x8ele du Nord-Ouest, \xc3\x8ele Observation, \xc3\x8ele Sud-Est and Ilot la Croix).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">Climate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Seychelles&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Climate">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The climate is equable although quite humid, as the islands are small,<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> classified by <a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen-Geiger_climate_classification_system" class="mw-redirect" title="K\xc3\xb6ppen-Geiger climate classification system">K\xc3\xb6ppen-Geiger system</a> as <a href="/wiki/Tropical_rain_forest" class="mw-redirect" title="Tropical rain forest">tropical rain forest</a> (Af). The temperature varies little throughout the year. Temperatures on Mah\xc3\xa9 vary from 24 to 30&#160;\xc2\xb0C (75 to 86&#160;\xc2\xb0F), and rainfall ranges from 2,900&#160;mm (114&#160;in) annually at <a href="/wiki/Victoria,_Seychelles" title="Victoria, Seychelles">Victoria</a> to 3,600&#160;mm (142&#160;in) on the mountain slopes. <a href="/wiki/Precipitation_(meteorology)" class="mw-redirect" title="Precipitation (meteorology)">Precipitation</a> is somewhat less on the other islands.<sup id="cite_ref-Climate_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Climate-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>During the coolest months, July and August, the average low is about 24&#160;\xc2\xb0C (75&#160;\xc2\xb0F). The southeast trade winds blow regularly from May to November, and this is the most pleasant time of the year. The hot months are from December to April, with higher humidity (80%). March and April are the hottest months, but the temperature seldom exceeds 31&#160;\xc2\xb0C (88&#160;\xc2\xb0F). Most of the islands lie outside the cyclone belt, so high winds are rare.<sup id="cite_ref-Climate_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Climate-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable collapsible" style="width:90%; text-align:center; font-size:90%; line-height: 1.2em; margin:auto;">\n\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="14">Climate data for Victoria (<a
